| play_VST_x64 | East West | C:\Program Files\Vstplugins\play_VST_x64.dll |
| play_VST_x64 | East West | C:\Program Files\VSTPlugins\play_VST_x64.dll |

## Organization Strategy (Recommended)

1. **Prioritize VST3**: VST3 is the modern standard. Keep your VST3 folder (C:\Program Files\Common Files\VST3) clean.
2. **Consolidate VST2**:
   - Create a single folder for VST2 plugins, e.g., C:\VstPlugins.
   - Move all scattered VST2 DLLs to this folder, organized by Vendor.
   - Update Cubase's VST2 Plugin Path settings to point ONLY to this folder.
3. **Remove Ghost Plugins**:
   - The 'Missing Plugins' list shows plugins Cubase expects but can't find.
   - Go to Cubase's **Plugin Manager** -> **Blocklist** and clear/refresh.
4. **32-bit vs 64-bit**: Cubase 11+ is 64-bit only. Delete any 32-bit (x86) DLLs.
